! File containing locations list for fieldextra
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
! File format:
! ------------
! All lines beginning with an exclamation mark are ignored. All other lines are interpreted.
! A location is defined by two lines:
!
! The first line is made up of the fields described below; any text added after these fields
! is ignored:
!   Id:            unique string defining location (must not contain any column)
!   Description:   description of the location (station name,...)
!   Region:        region description (e.g. used in LM_GPPA output for stations clustering)
!   Flags:         string consisting of 10 characters which can be individually set to the
!                  values 'Y' (yes), 'N' (no), and '_' (undefined),respectively, and which
!                  have the following meanings
!            Flags(1):    dd not representative
!            Flags(2):    ff not representative
!            Flags(3):    Kalman filter available
!            Flags(4-10): unused
!   Lon:           longitude of location, in (-180.0,180.0) [deg]
!   Lat:           latitude of location, in (-90.0,90.0) [deg]
!   Alt:           location altitude [m]
!   gpi/gpj:       index of associated LM grid point (automatic association if set to 0)
!   gph:           height of associated LM grid point (only if gpi/gpj explicitely specified)
!
! The second line is a comma-separated list of location aliases. These are unique strings of the form '<group>:<name>',
! which may be used in the namelist and LM_GP output alternatively to the station id. With these aliases it is
! possible to assign one location to several groups. In order to select data at all locations belonging to one particular
! group, it is sufficient to specify just the name of the group in the namelist.
! Each group specifier may only be used once within a list of aliases that are defined for a certain location.
!
! The second line is empty if no aliases are defined.
!
! ATTENTION: Fieldextra recognizes the group specifier 'WMO' and tries to interpret the
!            related location names as 5-digit WMO numbers. Thus one should use this
!            group specification consistently. The recognition of the string 'WMO' is
!            case-independent.
!
!Id         Description                              Region               Flag       Lon       Lat       Alt  gpi  gpj  gph
!A10        A40                                      A20                  A10        F9.4      F9.4      I4   I4   I4   I4
!aaaaaaaaaa aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa aaaaaaaaaa ffff.ffff ffff.ffff iiii iiii iiii iiii
!Aliases (comma separated list of strings of the form '<group>:<name>')
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
! ANETZ locations
